                        <div class="headline_area">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2013/06/coffee-caramels/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Coffee Caramels">Coffee
                            Caramels</a></h2>\n
                            <p class="headline_meta">by <span class=
                            "author vcard fn">Eddy Van Damme</span> on
                            <abbr class="published" title="2013-06-24">June 24,
                            2013</abbr></p>\n
                        </div>\n
                        <div class="format_text entry-content">
                            \n
                            <p>\xc2\xa0</p>\n
                            <p><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/06/Coffee-caramels.jpg">
                            <img alt="Coffee caramels" class=
                            "alignleft size-large wp-image-2295" height="680"
                            src=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/06/Coffee-caramels-1024x680.jpg"
                            width="1024" /></a></p>\n
                            <p>Caramels are much desired the world over and can
                            be made in many different flavors. While vanilla
                            and chocolate are the most popular ones, coffee
                            pairs exceptionally well with the buttery tones of
                            caramel.</p>\n
                            <p>The coffee caramels can be wrapped in cellophane
                            as shown in On Baking, or can be dipped in milk or
                            dark chocolate couverture and finished with a touch
                            of fleur de sel, if so desired.</p>\n
                            <p>Coffee Caramel</p>\n
                            <p>A chewy caramel that does not stick to
                            teeth.</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n
                            <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">
                                <tbody>
                                    <tr>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="210"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="109"></td>
                                    </tr>
                                    <tr>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160">1 x
                                        recipe</td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="210">Caramel
                                        candies, On Baking 3, page 730</td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="109">1 x
                                        recipe</td>
                                    </tr>
                                    <tr>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160">1.5
                                        oz</td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="210">Coffee
                                        extract</td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="109">45 g</td>
                                    </tr>
                                    <tr>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="210"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="109"></td>
                                    </tr>
                                    <tr>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160">
                                        \xc2\xa0</td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="210"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="109"></td>
                                    </tr>
                                    <tr>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="210"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="109"></td>
                                    </tr>
                                </tbody>
                            </table>\n
                            <p>\xc2\xa0</p>\n
                            <ol>
                                <li style="list-style: none">\n</li>
                                <li>Prepare recipe as indicated. Add coffee
                                extract at 245F (118C). Cook further until
                                caramel reaches 245F (118C) again. For a firmer
                                caramel cook a few degrees higher.\n</li>
                            </ol>\n
                            <p><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/06/caramels.jpg">
                            <img alt="caramels" class=
                            "alignleft size-large wp-image-2296" height="680"
                            src=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/06/caramels-1024x680.jpg"
                            width="1024" /></a></p>\n

                        <div class="headline_area">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2013/05/artisanal-belgian-chocolate-truffles/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Artisanal Belgian Chocolate Truffles">
                            Artisanal Belgian Chocolate Truffles</a></h2>\n
                            <p class="headline_meta">by <span class=
                            "author vcard fn">Eddy Van Damme</span> on
                            <abbr class="published" title="2013-05-20">May 20,
                            2013</abbr></p>\n
                        </div>\n
                        <div class="format_text entry-content">
                            \n
                            <p><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/Belgian-truffle-recipe.jpg">
                            <img alt="Belgian truffle recipe" class=
                            "alignleft wp-image-2282" height="544" src=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/Belgian-truffle-recipe-1024x680.jpg"
                            width="819" /></a></p>\n
                            <p>Truffles can be made either by using heavy
                            cream, chocolate and a sweetener or are made with
                            butter, chocolate and a sweetener. Both can be
                            delicious and have their own distinct
                            characteristic. If you desire to make truffles with
                            well pronounced flavor (from liquor, extracts, tea,
                            coffee etc) then butter based truffles may be a
                            good choice. The creamed butter mixture, which is
                            consequently light and airy makes it possible for
                            flavors to really shine through, which can be a
                            challenge when using bitter chocolate.</p>\n
                            <p>These truffles are flavored with homemade coffee
                            extract and sprinkled with nougatine.</p>\n
                            <p>Artisanal Belgian Truffles | Coffee
                            Nougatine</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n
                            <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">

                            <p>Yield: 60
                            truffles</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n

                                        butter, best quality</td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="109">250 g</td>
                                    </tr>
                                    <tr>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160">3 oz</td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="210"><a href=
                                        "http://www.chefeddy.com/2009/11/invert-sugar/"
                                        target="_blank">Invert sugar</a></td>
                                        <td valign="top" width="109">90 g</td>
                                    </tr>
                                    <tr>
                                        <td valign="top" width="160"></td>

                                        <td valign="top" width="109">750</td>
                                    </tr>
                                    <tr>

                            </table>\n
                            <ol>
                                <li style="list-style: none">\n</li>
                                <li>Mix butter until creamy, add invert sugar
                                and cream more.\n</li>
                                <li>Melt first listed dark and milk chocolate
                                to 95\xc2\xb0F (34\xc2\xb0C) and at this
                                temperature to creamed butter. Mix well and add
                                coffee extract and liquor and mix until
                                combined.\n</li>
                                <li>Let mixture set for approximately 30
                                minutes or until crystallization starts to take
                                place.\n</li>
                                <li>Pipe into even mounds. Sprinkle with very
                                thin rolled pieces of <a href=
                                "http://www.chefeddy.com/2009/10/nougatine/"
                                target="_blank">nougatine</a>. Do not place the
                                truffles in a refrigerator. Let set in a cool
                                area until fully crystallized, about 2
                                hours.\n</li>
                                <li>Temper couverture chocolate as shown on
                                this site and dip truffles, drop onto quality
                                cocoa powder.\n</li>
                                <li>Carefully roll the dipped truffles into
                                cocoa powder ensuring not to stick the fork
                                into the truffle itself.\n</li>
                                <li>When firm shake off extra cocoa powder and
                                place in a refrigerator. Serve at room
                                temperature for full flavor experience.\n</li>
                            </ol>\n
                            <p><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/Belgian-truffles.jpg">
                            <img alt="Belgian truffles" class=
                            "alignleft wp-image-2283" height="544" src=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/wp-content/uploads/2013/05/Belgian-truffles-1024x680.jpg"
                            width="819" /></a></p>\n
                            <p>\xc2\xa0</p>\n
                            <p>\xc2\xa0</p>\n
                            <p class="to_comments"><span class=
                            "bracket">{</span> <a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2013/05/artisanal-belgian-chocolate-truffles/#comments"
                            rel="nofollow"><span>18</span> comments</a>
                            <span class="bracket">}</span></p>\n
                        </div>\n
                    </div>\n

                            "teaser_date published" title="2013-03-04">March 4,
                            2013</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>While I lived in Belgium I was puzzled why
                                cinnamon was used in such large amounts in
                                baked goods in the United States. Later I
                                learned that the type of cinnamon used in North
                                America and many European countries differ.
                                American Pastry Chefs and Bakers mainly use
                                Korintje and Vietnamese
                                \xe2\x80\x9cSaigon\xe2\x80\x9d Cassia Cinnamon
                                while many [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                            "teaser_date published" title="2013-02-18">February

                                <p>Toasted hazelnuts deliver an incomparable
                                flavor to this shortbread. For optimum flavor,
                                toast hazelnuts in a medium temperature oven
                                until the heart of hazelnuts are golden brown.
                                I do not advise to grind hazelnuts in a food
                                processor without another ingredient present;
                                it most often leads to hazelnut paste. Adding
                                pastry flour to the toasted
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/08/egg-free-ice-cream-frangelico-ice-cream/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Egg Free Ice Cream | Frangelico Ice cream">
                            Egg Free Ice Cream | Frangelico Ice
                            cream</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2012-08-27">August 27, 2012</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>In ice cream, egg yolks are used for their
                                stabilizing ability as they bind water,
                                resulting in frozen desserts with a rich mouth
                                feel.\xc2\xa0 Large ice cream manufacturers
                                often use gums in addition to, or instead of
                                egg yolks. Gums allow hefty amounts of air
                                incorporation during churning, increasing the
                                volume of an ice cream [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/08/egg-free-ice-cream-frangelico-ice-cream/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n

                            Almond Petit Four |Lemon

                            "teaser_date published" title="2012-07-30">July 30,
                            2012</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Piped almond petit four are much appreciated
                                by our clients and certainly belong in a
                                luxurious assortment of petit four.\xc2\xa0
                                Sugar content in almond paste can vary
                                therefore it is very important to use the right
                                kind. Almond paste with high sugar content will
                                result in petit four which will spread out too
                                much during [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                        id="post-1815">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/03/raspberry-mint-sorbet/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Raspberry Mint Sorbet">Raspberry
                            Mint Sorbet</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2012-03-19">March
                            19, 2012</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Simple desserts do not necessarily translate
                                into boring. A minimal composition of raspberry
                                mint sorbet sandwiched between thin sheets of
                                cocoa nib topped chocolate is an example of
                                such. For most sorbets I recommend a
                                combination of sugars such as invert sugar,
                                glucose and granulated sugar. Invert sugar and
                                glucose along with pectin (or other
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/03/raspberry-mint-sorbet/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-1802 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-desserts-in-a-glass"
                        id="post-1802">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/03/noble-chocolate-cream/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Noble Chocolate Cream">Noble
                            Chocolate Cream</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2012-03-05">March 5,
                            2012</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Noble chocolate cream is a cousin of
                                chocolate cremeux but made without egg yolk.
                                Another difference is that it contains higher
                                amount of milk than whipping cream, this allows
                                the chocolate flavor to be fully pronounced.
                                (High fat content has a tendency to masks
                                flavors) Since no eggs are present and a
                                smaller amount of [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/03/noble-chocolate-cream/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                    </div>\n
                    <div class="prev_next">
                        \n
                        <p class="previous floated"><a href=
                        "http://www.chefeddy.com/page/4/">\xe2\x86\x90 Previous
                        Entries</a></p>\n
                        <p class="next"><a href=
                        "http://www.chefeddy.com/page/2/">Next Entries
                        \xe2\x86\x92</a></p>\n
                    </div>\n

                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=

                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>We all know that many plated desserts can go
                                from ordinary to extraordinary by simply adding
                                an eye catching tuile. It is the reason why so
                                many of us use them in our work on a daily
                                basis. Made round, square, into long strips,
                                curved, left flat, rolled, the possibilities
                                are nearly endless. Besides being
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/01/tuiles/" rel=
                            "nofollow">Read the full article \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                    </div>\n
                    <div class="teasers_box">
                        \n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser post-1755 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-ingredients"
                        id="post-1755">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/01/candied-kumquats/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Candied kumquats">Candied
                            kumquats</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2012-01-16">January
                            16, 2012</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Kumquats are some of the quickest and least
                                complicated fruits to candy. From start to
                                finish, semi candied kumquats can be achieved
                                within 40 minutes.\xc2\xa0 A drastic time
                                difference compared to the preparation of
                                candied orange peels which are blanched several
                                times to remove bitterness from the peel and
                                are then followed by an extensive
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/01/candied-kumquats/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-1740 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-tips-and-techniques"
                        id="post-1740">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/01/pate-a-choux-with-streusel/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to P\xc3\xa2te \xc3\xa0 Choux with Streusel">
                            P\xc3\xa2te \xc3\xa0 Choux with
                            Streusel</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2012-01-09">January
                            9, 2012</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>P\xc3\xa2te \xc3\xa0 Choux topped with
                                streusel or crumble has some real
                                advantages.\xc2\xa0 One, a smooth rounded
                                surface on profiteroles or \xc3\xa9clairs is
                                easily obtained. Two, the added flavor and
                                texture of streusel is a welcoming factor to
                                the rather bland flavor of P\xc3\xa2te \xc3\xa0
                                Choux. Three, profiteroles or \xc3\xa9clairs
                                expand much larger and more uniformly
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/01/pate-a-choux-with-streusel/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                    </div>\n
                    <div class="teasers_box">

                        <div class=
                        "teaser post-1732 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-chocolates"
                        id="post-1732">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/01/hazelnut-orange-chocolate-bar/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Hazelnut &amp; Orange Chocolate Bar">
                            Hazelnut &amp; Orange Chocolate
                            Bar</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2012-01-03">January 3, 2012</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>\xc2\xa0 After talking to countless Pastry
                                chefs and Chocolatiers who are in search of
                                fillings for chocolates with an extended shelf
                                life, I thought it was time to highlight such
                                filling which may be of use to you.\xc2\xa0
                                This particular filling contains nougatine
                                which adds a layer of complexity, but the good
                                news is that [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2012/01/hazelnut-orange-chocolate-bar/"

                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-1718 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-chocolates category-ingredients"
                        id="post-1718">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/12/gianduja/" rel=
                            "bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Gianduja">Gianduja</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2011-12-27">December 27, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>\xc2\xa0 Gianduja is a highly desired
                                filling for chocolates as it is both delicious
                                and luxurious. Many recipes and methods to
                                prepare Gianduja exist but all contain similar
                                ingredients. These mainly include hazelnuts,
                                sugar and chocolate and at times with lesser
                                amounts, milk powder and cocoa butter. Some of
                                us in the pastry lab also [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/12/gianduja/" rel=
                            "nofollow">Read the full article \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                    </div>\n
                    <div class="teasers_box">
                        \n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser post-1710 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-chocolates"
                        id="post-1710">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/12/chocolate-mints/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Chocolate Mints">Chocolate
                            Mints</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2011-12-12">December 12, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>There is something to be said to have
                                chocolates in your repertoire which hold a long
                                shelf life. It can make your work schedule a
                                lot easier since you can make these types of
                                chocolates well in advance of busy holidays.
                                \xc2\xa0\xc2\xa0One type of filling which will
                                certainly keep fresh for at least 6 months
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/12/chocolate-mints/"

                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>\xc2\xa0 \xc2\xa0 Although ginger is used in
                                the savory kitchen year round, it seems that
                                most of us in the pastry kitchen (especially in
                                the West) use it mainly during the fall and
                                winter season.\xc2\xa0 One of the things that I
                                like about ginger is that it can be very
                                effective in creating an aura
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-11-14">November
                            14, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>During this busy season who has time to read
                                an article? Nobody, so let\xe2\x80\x99s just go
                                straight to the recipe! Cheers! Pumpkin
                                Mascarpone Domes with Star Anise Maple Sauce
                                Prepare pumpkin cake and set aside. Prepare
                                mascarpone cream and fill in silicone molds
                                alternating with the cake. Serve with star
                                anise infused maple sauce. Leaves:
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                            7, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>\xc2\xa0 Not every country in the world is
                                fond of pumpkin desserts but for the places
                                which do, pumpkin cheesecake is a welcoming
                                finish to a good meal. A nice thing about using
                                pumpkin in cheesecake is that pumpkin makes
                                this dessert lighter in fat calories, enhances
                                the creaminess and makes the dessert very
                                fitting [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-10-10">October
                            10, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>It is not easy to find good quality coconut
                                milk which provides consistent results and has
                                an excellent coconut flavor.\xc2\xa0 Some
                                canned coconut milks are very fatty or thick,
                                others are very liquid without much flavor.
                                Coconut milk can also be prohibitive expensive
                                for use in coconut cream pies or other common
                                preparations.\xc2\xa0 Our vendors
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                            "Permanent link to Fudge Brownies">Fudge
                            Brownies</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-10-03">October
                            3, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Some people prefer cake-like brownies but
                                the majority of people in North America favor
                                fudge-like brownies.\xc2\xa0 Moist and gooey
                                with a deep and well balanced chocolate flavor.
                                \xc2\xa0Due to the richness this is not the
                                type of brownie you desire as a large piece.
                                \xc2\xa0I suggest you keep these under
                                refrigeration since at room temperature
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=

                                increase its flavor. \xc2\xa0Figs love to be in
                                company of honey, white chocolate, Rum,
                                Amaretto, mascarpone, oranges, toasted
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/06/quick-lime-curd/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Quick Lime Curd">Quick Lime
                            Curd</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2011-06-06">June 6, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>\xc2\xa0 For plated desserts I very much
                                make sure that the various elements are not too
                                scattered, preventing the consumer of having to
                                \xe2\x80\x9cwork\xe2\x80\x9d at the dessert
                                (Ensuring that every bite has a good balance).
                                Most of us like desserts which are multi
                                layered with zero effort during the
                                consumption. For example take an \xc3\xa9clair.
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/06/quick-lime-curd/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article

                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-1452 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-plated_dessert"
                        id="post-1452">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/lemon-sorbet-lemon-rose-geranium-sorbet/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Lemon Sorbet | Lemon Rose Geranium Sorbet">
                            Lemon Sorbet | Lemon Rose Geranium
                            Sorbet</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-05-30">May 30,
                            2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Few desserts refresh and excite our taste
                                buds as lemon sorbet. \xc2\xa0Lemon is
                                wonderful when paired within the citrus family
                                but can be equally as delicious when harmonized
                                with black or red currant, edible geranium,
                                ginger, apricot, milk chocolate and others.
                                \xc2\xa0Ginger, edible geranium and other
                                flowers or herbs are simply extracted into the
                                sorbet [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/lemon-sorbet-lemon-rose-geranium-sorbet/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n

                        <div class=
                        "teaser post-1441 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-ingredients category-tips-and-techniques"

                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/opaline-transparent-tuile/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Opaline | Transparent Tuile">Opaline
                            | Transparent Tuile</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-05-23">May 23,
                            2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>For many desserts, Opaline also known as a
                                transparent tuile can be an eye catching
                                decoration. It is easy to make and it can be
                                colored as well. Since the ingredients are
                                basically like a lollipop, opaline can be
                                flavored with herbs, spices, extracts etc.
                                \xc2\xa0Like most sugar products it is quickly
                                affected by humidity [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/opaline-transparent-tuile/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-1432 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-desserts-in-a-glass"
                        id="post-1432">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/white-chocolate-cremeux/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to White Chocolate Cremeux">White
                            Chocolate Cremeux</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-05-16">May 16,
                            2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>If there is one ingredient which Pastry
                                Chefs feel a bit uneasy about using in the
                                pastry kitchen, it must be white chocolate. We
                                know very well that many people consider white
                                chocolate not real chocolate and most of us are
                                not smitten with white chocolate the same way
                                as we are with milk and [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/white-chocolate-cremeux/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                    </div>\n

                        <div class=

                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/tuile-designs/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Tuile Designs">Tuile
                            Designs</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-05-09">May 9,
                            2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>\xc2\xa0 Certain plated desserts require a
                                touch of elegance which can be achieved by a
                                variety of means. One of them is a contemporary
                                tuile d\xc3\xa9cor. Easy and fast to make and
                                well liked by our guest. Getting It All
                                Together! Tuile decors will absorb humidity
                                quickly, therefore it is important to make
                                these daily [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/tuile-designs/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n

                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-1409 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-puff-pastry"
                        id="post-1409">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/arlettes/" rel=
                            "bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Arlettes">Arlettes</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2011-05-02">May 2, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>One of the things I like to prepare with
                                leftover puff pastry trimmings are arlettes.
                                Their lightness pairs perfectly with gelato,
                                sorbet or a good fruit soup/plate. While I am
                                writing this, I have arlettes by my side but no
                                gelato or sorbet, only good espresso, and I
                                must say it is quite delicious as
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/05/arlettes/" rel=
                            "nofollow">Read the full article \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                    </div>\n
                    <div class="teasers_box">
                        \n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser post-1403 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-petit-four"

                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=

                            "Permanent link to Petit Four | Lemon">Petit Four |
                            Lemon</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2011-03-29">March 29, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>\xc2\xa0 Serving Petit fours are often more
                                complicated than one would believe. How they
                                will be served is just one of the issues. At a
                                cocktail party where the guest usually have a
                                beverage in one hand, it is important to keep
                                in mind that they have little opportunity to
                                fuss with forks, spoons, napkins
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/03/petit-four-lemon/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n

                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Key to any good dessert is balance of
                                ingredients. Using too much of any component
                                can make any dessert unpleasant to eat. Unless
                                of course if you particularly love a certain
                                component. Take for example this individual
                                Mango tart. The ratio of this light and
                                delicate Breton Shortbread is rather high to
                                the ratio of [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-03-16">March
                            16, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Daily stresses and working in a Pastry lab
                                requires us to fuel our body very well. One of
                                my favorite ways is a good cold glass of
                                chocolate milk. Since I have not found any
                                product on the market which satisfies my desire
                                for a well pronounced chocolate flavor I simply
                                make my own mix. [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=

                                <p>Pastry Chefs have several options when it
                                comes down to making Puff pastry and oftentimes
                                will prepare the type which they are most
                                familiar with or which they most prefer.
                                Personally I have found that all types can
                                produce excellent results when the procedure is
                                properly followed. However based upon my
                                research I do believe [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                        <div class=
                        "teaser post-1345 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-tarts"
                        id="post-1345">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/02/strawberry-tarts-with-cassis-cremeux/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Strawberry Tarts with Cassis Cremeux">
                            Strawberry Tarts with Cassis
                            Cremeux</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-02-22">February
                            22, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Lately I have been preparing quite a few
                                tarts made with puff pastry. Sure, in a way
                                somewhat old fashioned and certainly far more
                                difficult to handle if compared to shortbread
                                style tart dough. However, I think that we can
                                all agree that most people find pure butter
                                puff pastry simply irresistible. It is one
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/02/strawberry-tarts-with-cassis-cremeux/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-1326 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-danish-breakfast"
                        id="post-1326">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/02/kouing-aman/" rel=
                            "bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Kouing Aman">Kouing
                            Aman</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2011-02-15">February 15, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>It is fair to say that most people find a
                                perfect pure butter croissant or a delectable
                                apple turnover simply irresistible. It is
                                partly about the texture, the buttery flakes,
                                the aroma and the desire for more. \xc2\xa0Like
                                nearly everyone, I am also a huge aficionado of
                                Palmiers. To me, Palmiers caramelized crust and
                                its [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/02/kouing-aman/" rel=

                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/02/valentine-dessert/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Valentine Dessert">Valentine
                            Dessert</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-02-01">February
                            1, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Valentine menus tend to be filling and
                                oftentimes rich. For such occasions I like to
                                select a dessert which is either light or is
                                very strong in flavor. This lemon and passion
                                fruit cream does the trick. If desired serve
                                with raspberry, champagne and rose or
                                blackberry sorbet. For the heart I made a lemon
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/02/valentine-dessert/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-1303 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-petit-four-sec"

                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/01/valentines-petit-four-sec/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Valentines Petit Four Sec">Valentines
                            Petit Four Sec</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-01-25">January
                            25, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>For the weeks leading up to the day of love,
                                I am sharing some of the things which I find of
                                interest and which could be possibilities to
                                serve on or before Valentine.
                                \xc2\xa0\xc2\xa0The first in the collection is
                                a shortbread finished with raspberry jam,
                                almond macaronade and chocolate. It is an
                                excellent petit four [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/01/valentines-petit-four-sec/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n

                        <div class=
                        "teaser post-1294 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-cake"
                        id="post-1294">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/01/cheesecake-made-with-steviacane/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Cheesecake made with SteviaCane">
                            Cheesecake made with
                            SteviaCane</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-01-18">January
                            18, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>At times a pastry chef has to make desserts
                                which address certain dietary needs. Sometimes
                                the product needs to be without gluten,
                                lactose, salt or it may require having high
                                fiber content. Some people chose or by
                                doctor\xe2\x80\x99s order need to reduce their
                                sugar intake. Making ingredient changes in
                                desserts can be easy or challenging.
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/01/cheesecake-made-with-steviacane/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-1275 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-entremet-tortes"
                        id="post-1275">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/01/gateau-ferrini/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to G\xc3\xa2teau Ferrini">G\xc3\xa2teau
                            Ferrini</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2011-01-04">January
                            4, 2011</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Some of the finest cakes in the pastry shop
                                oftentimes contain almonds. Just to name a few:
                                Financier, Dacquoise, Pain de Genes, and
                                Joconde\xe2\x80\xa6. Indeed they are some of a
                                pastry chef most beloved cake layers to work
                                with. \xc2\xa0For this particular g\xc3\xa2teau
                                I used biscuit joconde as it allows me to
                                moisten it with [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2011/01/gateau-ferrini/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n

                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=

                            "Permanent link to Red Grapefruit Marmalade">Red
                            Grapefruit Marmalade</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2010-12-28">December
                            28, 2010</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>It\xe2\x80\x98s no wonder that the botanical
                                name for grapefruit is Citrus Paradisi. The
                                scent, the flavor, the cholesterol lowering
                                properties and the endless list of healthy
                                attributes make it a fruit straight from
                                paradise indeed. Grapefruit is one of the
                                fruits I love to use in desserts since it
                                brings an unmatched flavor to countless
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=

                            "teaser_date published" title="2010-12-23">December

                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>This past summer Lieve Blancquaert and her
                                amazing crew came to Houston and filmed me
                                nonstop for 4 days for an episode of her
                                beautiful documentary, titled \xe2\x80\x9cMade
                                in Belgium\xe2\x80\x9d. It\xe2\x80\x99s a
                                series of 8 shows, each featuring a chef who
                                works somewhere in the world. Her program took
                                her to South America, Africa, North
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n

                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2010/12/macaron/" rel=
                            "bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Macaron">Macaron</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2010-12-14">December 14, 2010</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>A fruit which never seems to escape my
                                interest are cranberries. I adore them in
                                savory applications as well as in
                                desserts.\xc2\xa0 Their acidic bitterness is
                                particularly welcome in desserts which are by
                                nature sweet and are in dire need of a touch of
                                balance. Think for example of wonderful baked
                                meringue layered with cranberry
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2010/12/macaron/" rel=
                            "nofollow">Read the full article \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n

                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2010/11/brioche/" rel=
                            "bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Brioche">Brioche</a></h2>\n<abbr class="teaser_date published"
                            title="2010-11-30">November 30, 2010</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Brioche with candied Buddha hand toasted
                                hazelnuts Good quality butter, a few ordinary
                                ingredients and close attention to detail can
                                make a most extraordinary brioche. The brioche
                                I feature here is made with a sponge and
                                therefore may not be as convenient to prepare,
                                compared to a brioche where the dough is
                                matured overnight in [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2010/11/brioche/" rel=
                            "nofollow">Read the full article \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n

                        <div class=
                        "teaser teaser_right post-948 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-plated_dessert"
                        id="post-948">
                            \n
                            <h2 class="entry-title"><a href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2010/07/belgian-waffles/"
                            rel="bookmark" title=
                            "Permanent link to Belgian Waffles">Belgian
                            Waffles</a></h2>\n<abbr class=
                            "teaser_date published" title="2010-07-14">July 14,
                            2010</abbr>\n
                            <div class="format_teaser entry-content">
                                \n
                                <p>Golden crispy on the outside, tender and
                                moist on the inside with a near see thru
                                appearance are the characteristics of a perfect
                                waffle. In Belgium, this type of waffle is
                                known as the Brussels waffle where it is very
                                popular. The Belgian or Brussels waffle was
                                first introduced in 1856 at the fair in
                                [\xe2\x80\xa6]</p>\n
                            </div>\n<a class="teaser_link" href=
                            "http://www.chefeddy.com/2010/07/belgian-waffles/"
                            rel="nofollow">Read the full article
                            \xe2\x86\x92</a>\n
                        </div>\n
                    </div>\n
                    <div class="prev_next">
                        \n
